### [262] [Can a Learner Regret Using a No-Regret Algorithm? A Control-Theoretic Study of Performance Dominance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03173)
*Hassan Abdelraouf,Jeff S. Shamma*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文研究了无悔学习算法中的“免费午餐”现象，即是否存在一种无悔算法能在所有支付环境中一致优于另一种无悔算法。研究人员将广义复制动态（RD）建模为一个线性时不变（LTI）系统与softmax非线性的级联。通过改变LTI系统，可以实现不同形式的RD，包括标准RD、预期RD等。研究发现，预期RD在所有支付环境中全局优于标准RD，证明了无悔学习动态中存在“免费午餐”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然无悔学习保证了学习者最终能获得不差于任何固定策略的平均奖励，但这个保证并没有确定最终的平均奖励值。不同的无悔学习动态在面对相同环境时，可能会产生不同的最终平均奖励。这促使研究者探索是否存在一种无悔算法能够在所有支付环境中一致优于另一种无悔算法，即是否存在“免费午餐”现象。

Method: 该研究将广义复制动态（RD）建模为一个线性时不变（LTI）系统与softmax非线性的级联。通过修改LTI系统，可以得到不同形式的RD，如标准RD、预期RD等。研究人员首先通过将性能比较形式化为关联比较系统的被动性（passivity）性质，建立了“局部”优势结果。然后，他们将预期RD与标准RD的性能比较转化为一个最优控制问题，并证明了最小可实现的累积奖励差距为零，从而建立了预期RD在所有支付环境下的全局优势，即“免费午餐”。

Result: 研究表明，通过修改LTI系统可以实现不同形式的广义复制动态。通过将性能比较视为一个被动性问题，研究人员证明了在平衡支付向量附近，一些RD形式具有“局部”优势。更重要的是，通过最优控制问题分析，证明了预期RD与标准RD之间的最小累积奖励差距为零，这意味着预期RD在所有支付环境中都优于标准RD，即存在“免费午餐”。

Conclusion: 本文通过将广义复制动态建模为LTI系统与softmax非线性的级联，证明了在无悔学习算法中存在“免费午餐”现象。具体而言，一种形式的预期RD在所有支付环境中均能一致优于标准RD，从而为无悔学习算法的性能比较提供了新的见解。

Abstract: No-regret learning dynamics ensure that a learner asymptotically achieves an average reward no worse than that of any fixed strategy. This no-regret guarantee does not determine the value of the asymptotic average reward. Indeed, it is possible for different no-regret learning dynamics to exhibit different asymptotic average rewards when facing the same environment while both assure the no-regret guarantee. This paper asks whether a "free-lunch" phenomenon can arise among no-regret algorithms. Namely, is it possible for one no-regret learning rule to uniformly outperform another no-regret learning rule across all payoff environments. Stated differently, can a learner regret not using a particular no-regret algorithm? We consider generalized replicator dynamics (RD) as a cascade interconnection between a linear time-invariant (LTI) system and the softmax nonlinearity. Varying this LTI system leads to different realizations of replicator dynamics, including so-called anticipatory RD, exponential RD, and other forms of higher-order RD. Setting the LTI system to be an integrator realizes standard RD, which is known to satisfy the no-regret property. Within this framework, we analyze and compare various realizations of these generalized realizations RD by varying the LTI system. We first formulate performance comparison as a passivity property of an associated comparison system and establish "local" dominance results, i.e., comparing the asymptotic performance near an equilibrium payoff vector. We then cast performance comparison between a form of anticipatory RD and standard RD as an optimal-control problem. We show that the minimal achievable cumulative reward gap is zero, thereby establishing global dominance of anticipatory RD across all payoff environments and establishing a "free lunch" among no-regret learning dynamics.

</details>

Our experiments demonstrate that LDAM with deferred re-weighting (LDAM-DRW) consistently outperforms standard BCE and asymmetric losses for rare class recognition. Amongst the architectures evaluated, ConvNeXt-Large achieves the best single-model performance with 0.5220 mAP and 0.3765 F1 on our development set, whilst classifier re-training and test-time augmentation further improve ranking metrics. On the official test leaderboard, our submission achieved 0.3950 mAP, ranking 5th amongst all 68 participating teams with total of 1528 submissions. Method: DLIOS采用三层透明窗口架构，配合事件驱动的WebView2捕获管道和线程安全的事件总线。关键技术包括：基于歌词元数据的分段式LLM广播自动化（生成电台风格评论）、支持热插拔的RadioPersonaConfig模式、实时弹幕快速响应引擎（关键词路由至预设语音或LLM生成回复），以及一个名为Suwan Li的AI歌手创作人案例研究。

Result: 经过36小时的压力测试，DLIOS实现了零弹幕重叠、零死锁崩溃；礼物特效P95延迟低于180毫秒；LLM到TTS的片段P95延迟低于2.1秒；TTS集成的响度增益达到9.5 LUFS。Suwan Li案例研究中，AI共生成了超过100首歌曲。

Conclusion: DLIOS成功地构建了一个LLM增强的实时多模态交互直播系统，该系统能够实现自动化的情感连贯评论、即时响应用户互动、支持多虚拟人播报，并提高了直播内容的吸引力。该系统在性能和稳定性方面表现出色。

Abstract: We present DLIOS, a Large Language Model (LLM)-augmented real-time multi-modal interactive enhancement overlay system for Douyin (TikTok) live streaming. DLIOS employs a three-layer transparent window architecture for independent rendering of danmaku (scrolling text), gift and like particle effects, and VIP entrance animations, built around an event-driven WebView2 capture pipeline and a thread-safe event bus. On top of this foundation we contribute an LLM broadcast automation framework comprising: (1) a per-song four-segment prompt scheduling system (T1 opening/transition, T2 empathy, T3 era story/production notes, T4 closing) that generates emotionally coherent radio-style commentary from lyric metadata; (2) a JSON-serializable RadioPersonaConfig schema supporting hot-swap multi-persona broadcasting; (3) a real-time danmaku quick-reaction engine with keyword routing to static urgent speech or LLM-generated empathetic responses; and (4) the Suwan Li AI singer-songwriter persona case study -- over 100 AI-generated songs produced with Suno. A 36-hour stress test demonstrates: zero danmaku overlap, zero deadlock crashes, gift effect P95 latency <= 180 ms, LLM-to-TTS segment P95 latency <= 2.1 s, and TTS integrated loudness gain of 9.5 LUFS. live streaming; danmaku; large language model; prompt engineering; virtual persona; WebView2; WINMM; TTS; Suno; loudness normalization; real-time scheduling

</details>


### [266] [Context Adaptive Extended Chain Coding for Semantic Map Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03073)
*Runyu Yang,Junqi Liao,Hyomin Choi,Fabien Racapé,Ivan V. Bajić*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于链码的无损语义图压缩框架，通过利用轮廓拓扑和共享边界，以及上下文自适应熵编码和跳过编码机制，实现了比现有方法更高的压缩率和更快的编解码速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着语义图在机器人、自动驾驶和扩展现实等领域的广泛应用，需要高效的压缩方法来保留其结构化的语义信息。

Method: 提出了一种扩展链码（ECC）来表示轮廓，并保留了传统的3OT链码作为回退。采用基于马尔可夫模型的上下文自适应熵编码方案。引入了跳过编码机制来处理相邻语义区域之间的共享轮廓，支持完全跳过和部分跳过。

Result: 在语义图数据集上，平均比特率降低了18%。编解码器运行时分别减少了98%和50%。在占用图上的评估也显示出一致的压缩增益。

Conclusion: 提出的方法能够有效地无损压缩语义图，在压缩率和效率方面优于现有基准方法，并且在不同类型的地图上表现出一致的性能。

Abstract: Semantic maps are increasingly utilized in areas such as robotics, autonomous systems, and extended reality, motivating the investigation of efficient compression methods that preserve structured semantic information. This paper studies lossless compression of semantic maps through a novel chain-coding-based framework that explicitly exploits contour topology and shared boundaries between adjacent semantic regions. We propose an extended chain code (ECC) to represent long-range contour transitions more compactly, while retaining a legacy three-orthogonal chain code (3OT) as a fallback mode for further efficiency. To efficiently encode sequences of ECC symbols, a context-adaptive entropy coding scheme based on Markov modeling is employed. Furthermore, a skip-coding mechanism is introduced to eliminate redundant representations of shared contours between adjacent semantic regions, supporting both complete and partial skips via run-length signaling. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method achieves an average bitrate reduction of 18\% compared with a state-of-the-art benchmark on semantic map datasets. In addition, the proposed encoder and decoder achieve up to 98\% and 50\% runtime reduction, respectively, relative to a modern generic lossless codec. Extended evaluations on occupancy maps further confirm consistent compression gains across the majority of tested scenarios.

</details>
